#inflation_early control to reduce money supply lategame
#id4760040 Messures the current inflation_early level
#id4760041 Turns worldbank off (timed via levels)
#id4760042 Turns worldbank on (timed via levels)
#id4760043 Sets the World bank control level
#
#
country_event = {
    id = 4760044
    title = "Test Event"
    desc = "This is a test event that gives the country the 'test' modifier."

    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = { 
        1112 = { secede_province = LCT change_controller = LCT }
        LCT = { capital = 1112 }
        3252 = { secede_province = GHO }
    }

    option = {
        3252 = { secede_province = LCT }
        LCT = { capital = 3252 }        
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = 4760045

    desc = "This is a test event that gives the country the 'test' modifier."

    is_triggered_only = yes

    immediate = { 
    }

    option = {
        LCT = { build_factory_in_capital_state = world_bank_factory }  
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = 4760041
    title = "Bank turns off"
    desc = "This is an attempt at stopping inflation_early"
    picture = "dixie"
    
	trigger = {
		tag = GHO
		has_country_flag = bank_on
		NOT = { has_country_flag = bank_off }
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_1
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_2 }
				Month = 1
				NOT = { Month = 3 }
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_2
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_3 }
				Month = 1
				NOT = { Month = 5 }
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_3
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_4 }
				Month = 1
				NOT = { Month = 7 }
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_4
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_5 }
				Month = 1
				NOT = { Month = 9 }
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_5
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_6 }
				Month = 1
				NOT = { Month = 11 }
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_6
				OR = {
					Month = 0
					Month = 1
					Month = 2
					Month = 3
					Month = 4
					Month = 5
					Month = 6
					Month = 7
					Month = 8
					Month = 9
					Month = 10
					Month = 11
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	immediate = { 
		GHO = { 
			clr_country_flag = bank_on
	    	set_country_flag = bank_off
	    }
	}

    option = {
        name = "Lights Off"
		GHO = {
			country_event = { id=4760044 days=0 }
		}
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = 4760042
    title = "Bank turns on"
    desc = "This was an attempt at stopping inflation_early"
    picture = "dixie"
    
	trigger = {
		tag = GHO
		has_country_flag = bank_off
		NOT = { has_country_flag = bank_on }
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_1 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_2 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_3 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_4 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_5 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_6 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ED_1 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ED_2 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ED_3 }
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_1
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_2 }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						Month = 0
						NOT = { Month = 1 }
					}
					AND = {
						Month = 3
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_2
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_3 }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						Month = 0
						NOT = { Month = 1 }
					}
					AND = {
						Month = 5
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_3
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_4 }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						Month = 0
						NOT = { Month = 1 }
					}
					AND = {
						Month = 7
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_4
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_5 }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						Month = 0
						NOT = { Month = 1 }
					}
					AND = {
						Month = 9
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = WB_5
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WB_6 }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						Month = 0
						NOT = { Month = 1 }
					}
					AND = {
						Month = 11
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	immediate = { 
		clr_country_flag = bank_off
		set_country_flag = bank_on
		}

    option = {
        name = "Lights On"
		GHO = {
			country_event = { id=4760045 days=0 }
		}
    }
}

country_event = {
	id = 4760050
	title = "inflation_early check"
	desc = "Prevents some issues down the road"
	picture = "dixie"

		tag = GHO
		Month = 0
		NOT = { Month = 1 }
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = inflation_early_check_done }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	immediate = {
		GHO = { 
			set_variable = { which = inflation_early value = 0.001 }

				name = inflation_early_check_done

		}
	}

			}

		}
		any_country = {
			Limit = {
				AND = {
					Money = 100000

					rank = 1
					NOT = { rank = 0 }
				}
			}

country_event = {
	id = 4760043
	title = "Flatline Check"
	desc = "This is supposed to make the money decline gradual"
	picture = "dixie"
	
	trigger = {
		tag = GHO
		Month = 11
		NOT = { Month = 0 }
		NOT = { has_country_modifier = inflation_late_check_done }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	immediate = {
		GHO = { 
			set_variable = { which = inflation_late value = 0.001 }

				name = inflation_late_check_done
				duration = 40
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
